<div id="review_224171067" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/224171067" />
    <a title="Tilly Slaton" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6289182-tilly-slaton"><img alt="Tilly Slaton" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/224171067?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tilly Slaton" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tilly Slaton" href="/user/show/6289182-tilly-slaton">Tilly Slaton</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6289182-tilly-slaton?shelf=reviews-completed">reviews-completed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer224171067" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer548382125503638601">Night Play is the Dark-Hunter story of Vane and Bride.<br/><br/>This is one of my favorite stories in this series. Their relationship is inspiring and I found myself holding my breath as I read through wonderfully intimate (sexual and non-sexual) scenes.<br/><br/>Vane is a wolf. The whole story behind him is a bit complex so I will leave well enough alone! He’s a wolf. He’s a man. He’s sexy. Bottom line. Betrayed by their father, Vane and Fang are left hanging from a tree. If the alligators don’t get them, the Daim</span>
  <span id="freeText548382125503638601" style="display:none">Night Play is the Dark-Hunter story of Vane and Bride.<br /><br />This is one of my favorite stories in this series. Their relationship is inspiring and I found myself holding my breath as I read through wonderfully intimate (sexual and non-sexual) scenes.<br /><br />Vane is a wolf. The whole story behind him is a bit complex so I will leave well enough alone! He’s a wolf. He’s a man. He’s sexy. Bottom line. Betrayed by their father, Vane and Fang are left hanging from a tree. If the alligators don’t get them, the Daimons will.<br /><br />Bride is a curvy woman with more kindness beating through her veins than an entire city. Unfortunately, being a size 18 woman, men have treated her poorly. The bastards. Her boyfriend breaks up with her via letter that was delivered to her and charged to her account. Just imagine being dumped with your own pennies.<br /><br />Angry and crying as she cleaned her store, Vane walked by and *drum roll* his heart stopped at the sight of her. Unlike most relationships, this one has far less struggle. He likes her. She likes him. There isn’t a whole ton of what ifs during the foundation stage.<br /><br /><i>She couldn’t imagine this guy having trouble getting any woman he wanted. Who on earth would say no to that? On second thought, she hoped she never met a woman who attractive. If she did, she would be morally obligated to run her over in her car.</i><br /><br />Left for dead, his brother, Fang is comatose. Once their pack realizes that Vane and Fang are indeed still alive, they fan out in search for them. Hiding isn’t so easy when scents are involved.<br /><br />After making love to Bride, mating marks are seared into their palms. The meaning is unknown to Bride. To Vane, time is now against him. He only has so much time for Bride to accept him as her mate before he is doomed to an eternity of impotence. Imagine all of that .. with a nice healthy dose of hiding from a pack of rabid wolves <br /><br /><i>“I never knew softness,” he breathed. “Not until the moment you touched me in your store. My life is violent and dangerous. It’s dark and twisted and no place for someone like you. I have more people wanting me dead than I can count. They will stop at nothing and you…” He ground his teeth before he spoke again. “You’ll never want again for anything in your life. I swear it on what little bit of human soul I have left.”</i><br /><br />This book is fast! This book is fun! This book is amazing!<br /><br />I recommend this book to all mature adults in need of a good read. Semi-severe violence including discussion of gang rape (little description). Moderately delicious sexual content. This book will not disappoint!<br /><br />Line of the book:<br /><br /><i>The only way to have eternal love is to never let your heart forget what it’s like to live without it.</i><br /><br />~Happy reading!<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="548382125503638601" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_163758218" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/163758218" />
    <a title="Myvampfiction" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5326777-myvampfiction"><img alt="Myvampfiction" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1316103743p2/5326777.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/163758218?book_show_action=true">Apr 26, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Myvampfiction" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Myvampfiction" href="/user/show/5326777-myvampfiction">Myvampfiction</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer163758218" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8491418148401838616">review by Meesh<br/><br/>*Warning: possible spoilers ahead.*<br/><br/>Tastes change a lot as a woman ages. When we're young and reckless, lots of us look at just the outer package. We want the flash. We want sexy and successful. A lot of young women will ignore a lot of very bad habits in men if they're good looking enough, drive a great car (or in my case, motorcycle), or have enough money. Then we grow up, which a lot of us feel is a very good thing. But what isn't good is the impetus for maturing.<br/><br/>Let me be a lit</span>
  <span id="freeText8491418148401838616" style="display:none">review by Meesh<br /><br />*Warning: possible spoilers ahead.*<br /><br />Tastes change a lot as a woman ages. When we're young and reckless, lots of us look at just the outer package. We want the flash. We want sexy and successful. A lot of young women will ignore a lot of very bad habits in men if they're good looking enough, drive a great car (or in my case, motorcycle), or have enough money. Then we grow up, which a lot of us feel is a very good thing. But what isn't good is the impetus for maturing.<br /><br />Let me be a little personal here. I used to go after bad boys with "problems". I just knew I could fix them, make them better, and then they would love me. My mom said I was out to save the world one loser at a time. The problem with that is those kinds of guys can't be fixed, and they really seem to love to spread their poison to anyone who tries to get close to them. One loser in particular stands out in my memory, and he was every reason my taste in men changed. <br /><br />Not that he was particularly hot or sexy, but being lovestruck, I thought he was. Tattoed, long hair, high school drop out. He treated me like dirt under his shoes and I begged him for more. After being told I was fat one too many times, and that I wasn't pretty enough, and that maybe if I would stop acting so damn smart he would love me, a light bulb went off in my head. Epiphany is hard to spell, but even harder to recognize. After five years of torment, I finally had enough bad boy to last me the rest of my life.<br /><br />So what does this have to do with the book review? I'm sure you're all dying to know. Night Play is a Dark Hunter book, and it is my favorite. Bride, the lead female, had a boyfriend who treated her poorly. She wasn't a size 6, perfect little cookie cutter woman, and he made sure she knew it. He would make comments about her weight, what she was eating, and finally, he dumped her in a most degrading way. He wrote her a letter, basically telling her he needed someone better than she could ever be. I know how it feels to be told something like that, and I immediately felt her humiliation. So after a long relationship of being told all these bad things about herself, she didn't really see herself as attractive and worthy of love from a good man.<br /><br />Vane Kattalakis was a man (well, a wolf really) who saw more than just the good in her. She was the most beautiful woman to him. From the moment he saw her, he was drawn to Bride in a way he couldn't understand. Of course, as a were-hunter, Vane had his own hang ups and family issues. Growing up in a pack of wolves, he had very different socialization experiences than humans and wasn't exactly sure how humans courted.<br /><br />Their first meeting was the kind of encounter that would make even an unromantic person like me giddy. I guess I should say it did make even an unromantic person like me giddy. Vane went into Bride's store, bought a beautiful - and expensive - necklace, had her gift wrap it, and then walked away, leaving it on the counter. She yelled after him that he forgot it and his response melted my heart. "No, I left it with the woman I wanted to have it." Then he made a comment about how beautiful women should have beautiful things, and because Bride was so unaccustomed to hearing anyone say that she was beautiful, she started crying. He made it all better by taking her into the dressing room and making wild love to her. Awesome first sex scene.<br /><br />Throughout the book, Bride continually questions why this very sexy man would want someone so imperfect. When the man who unceremoniously dumped her decided to try to cause problems for her, Vane came to her rescue in a way that brought out my love for bad boys again, not that I ever truly lost that spark, really. The fates had decided that Vane and Bride were destined to be mates, human and were-hunter, and it was so endearing to watch Vane protect her until she could trust that his attraction and love for her were genuine. He healed a lot of gaping wounds left by years of being told she was less than because she wasn't our society's ideal.<br /><br />Of course, there are hot scenes throughout the entire book, and the description of Vane makes me a little breathless. Ponytail, tight t-shirt, all those things I left behind, only in a character who isn't another loser to be saved from himself. Vane knew how to treat the woman he adored, and that is really how every woman deserves to be treated. Sure, not all the time because let's face it. If our men were erect for us 24/7 and we responded in kind, work would never get done and the human race would perish from starvation, albeit the end would be lusty enough that I'm pretty sure I wouldn't even notice the hunger.<br /><br />Most of the Dark Hunter books are good, but I think like the Brothers, there are hunters each woman will be drawn to for different reasons. Vane is the hunter that touched me the most, and his mate was a woman I really liked too. If I could live in these books, I would and I recommend them to everyone I know. So go read them and then we'll have another common set of warriors to slobber over, ladies.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8491418148401838616" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer210729802404872727">My first ever DH book, I can't believe it:) it feels like... well last year haha, way back when I don't know there's a Goodreads site...happy memories:)<br/><br/>There's so much information on who, what, where and how these characters came from especially the Hero, but it was explained in every detailed in the beginning,which got me interested in the first place. So...I won't going to tackle that anymore but I'll make some rambling thoughts about the Hero and Heroine and also why I love this book!:)<br/><br/>I love</span>
  <span id="freeText210729802404872727" style="display:none">My first ever DH book, I can't believe it:) it feels like... well last year haha, way back when I don't know there's a Goodreads site...happy memories:)<br /><br />There's so much information on who, what, where and how these characters came from especially the Hero, but it was explained in every detailed in the beginning,which got me interested in the first place. So...I won't going to tackle that anymore but I'll make some rambling thoughts about the Hero and Heroine and also why I love this book!:)<br /><br />I love Vane, such a genuine man, he is an Alpha male alright who always takes care of his Lady and protect her when trouble snaps out of nowhere. He will fight whoever is going to hurt his mate.<br />I adore Bride, she is very different from the Author's other heroines because of her physical attributes, she's "Rubenesque" like. which was kinda refreshing from those lean and sexy woman out there, but Bride carries herself with grace although sometimes she felt insecure on her weight but Vane is always there to say, that he won't let anything change from her and that he loves her flaws and all *sigh* and oh she can kick <s>ass</s> too even if its her mother-in-law she's butt kicking;)<br /><br />This book was sweet, with humor, sarcasm, some swoon worthy scenes and fight scenes from enemies...its a little bit fluffy though compared to the other books but wa hey its my first book in the series, I've been enthralled by the universe the Author made, and I'm addicted to it!:)♥<br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11510884736539425604">Different from the other Dark-Hunter novels. This is the first of the Were-Hunter series, but if you follow the author's reading list this is #9. <br/><br/>How this differs from the DH novels: No serious big bad or end of the world problems. Vane does have people after him, but it's not an all consuming problem. The main point of the story is Vane winning/wooing Bride. <br/><br/>Vane saw Bride months again & was floored by her beauty. She's a rubenesque lady who owns a lingerie/clothing boutique & was just dumped b</span>
  <span id="freeText11510884736539425604" style="display:none">Different from the other Dark-Hunter novels. This is the first of the Were-Hunter series, but if you follow the author's reading list this is #9. <br /><br />How this differs from the DH novels: No serious big bad or end of the world problems. Vane does have people after him, but it's not an all consuming problem. The main point of the story is Vane winning/wooing Bride. <br /><br />Vane saw Bride months again &amp; was floored by her beauty. She's a rubenesque lady who owns a lingerie/clothing boutique &amp; was just dumped by her pretentious bf for not being a size 2. Vane re-encounters her the day she's dumped &amp; comforts her. They begin dating, sort of, and the rest of the story is their relationship, Vane dealing with family problems, &amp; trying to figure out how to tell Bride he's a werewolf...or if he should leave her out of his supernatural world. <br /><br />It's a sweet story &amp; a nice change of pace from the regular DH stories of world doom. I liked both characters, Bride is a very normal female &amp; Vane is swoony with his wish to do anything to make her happy.</span>

<div id="review_102539420" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/102539420" />
    <a title="Julie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2691297-julie"><img alt="Julie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1331223010p2/2691297.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/102539420?book_show_action=true">May 12, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Julie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Julie" href="/user/show/2691297-julie">Julie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2691297-julie?shelf=read-in-2010">read-in-2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2691297-julie?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer102539420" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2885091626076912075">Vane. That is one name that often comes up when I mention to people that I am reading Sherrilyn Kenyon’s Dark-Hunter series. “Oh that Vane, he’s so hot!”, “Oh that Vane, he’s so dreamy!”, “Oh that Vane, he can take me up against a tree and growl in my ear any day!” Ooookay then… So, after hearing that, I was quite excited to finally be reading about the infamous Vane Kattalakis, the wolf man, in “Night Play”.<br/><br/>It was nice to step away from the “vampire” Dark-Hunter world and explore the shape shif</span>
  <span id="freeText2885091626076912075" style="display:none">Vane. That is one name that often comes up when I mention to people that I am reading Sherrilyn Kenyon’s Dark-Hunter series. “Oh that Vane, he’s so hot!”, “Oh that Vane, he’s so dreamy!”, “Oh that Vane, he can take me up against a tree and growl in my ear any day!” Ooookay then… So, after hearing that, I was quite excited to finally be reading about the infamous Vane Kattalakis, the wolf man, in “Night Play”.<br /><br />It was nice to step away from the “vampire” Dark-Hunter world and explore the shape shifter part of this series in Vane’s book. You don’t leave the world you’ve come to love at all. You still see Kyrian, Amanda and Nick too (which was fun), but you really get a good look into the Were-Hunter world. All the different animals that shift to human forms and the politics behind them. Sherrilyn has put such thought in her worlds that you can’t help but be impressed with the amount of specifics there are. And I like that most are animals that shift to human and not the other way around like is the norm in paranormal books. Very inventive.<br /><br />Vane is a wolf. He and his brother Fang have been exiled and sentenced to die by their father thanks to an event that occurred back in book two. As with all the heroes in Sherrilyn’s books, Vane’s past sucked. But in comparison, it’s not so bad! I was glad to get a little reprieve from the gut-wrenching storyline. Yes, Vane’s mother wants him dead because his father beat her and his father wants him dead because…well because he’s an a**. Yes, Vane’s brother is in a coma of sorts and his sister was recently murdered. But, believe it or not, that’s a walk in the park compared to some of the other main guys in this series. So that too was a nice change of pace. Vane is a little lost in the human world, and is very lost when he discovers that Bride, a human, is his fated mate. He doesn’t know how to court a human female, let alone make love to one (he’s used to wolf-doggie style if you know what I’m saying *wink wink*)! But he is such a sweetheart! Following his instincts to protect his mate, he takes perfect care of Bride and makes her feel loved and cherished. *sigh*<br /><br />I really though Bride was a sweet character too. These two are just so sweet together! (Hmm, how many times can I use the word ‘sweet’ in one review?) Bride is not a super skinny super model. I really admire authors who ‘go there’. Who make their heroines what might be considered by some as physically flawed, also known as normal! She’s a little chubby, always has been. She’s always been around men who are always telling her to lose weight. Until Vane that is. He makes her eat cake! I mean, how romantic is that!? And he does it in front of her mommy! *swoon* Bride is compassionate and wholesome. No strange or paranormal stuff in this lady’s past. So the fact that Vane is a wolf and that there is a whole ‘other’ world out there doesn’t come easy to her. I like that too. Sometimes I think that the heroes or heroines are just a little too accommodating, too accepting. It’s like “You’re a what?! You mean they really do exist and they are deadly and all the things you read about? Oh hell, whatever. You’re good in bed so let’s spend the rest of our lives together…” Okay, yeah. Bride is torn as to what to do and it’s refreshing to see a nice, normal gal dealing with not at all normal stuff in a nice normal fashion. I think Sherrilyn did a great job here. And I love Bride with Vane. Yet another wonderful match.<br /><br />Now, as in every one of my past Dark-Hunter reviews, I must talk about Acheron. In “Night Play”, we see Ash interacting with Marissa, Kyrian and Amanda’s little baby girl. Now, if I didn’t already go all mushy wushy over Ash ever time he graced the page, that made it happen ten fold. Ash is amazing and I CAN’T WAIT TO GET TO HIS BOOK! (Acheron is book #15. Fifteen!!!) And Simi, his Demon companion is a riot! I really enjoy her. She always puts a smile on my face, especially how she makes grown men cringe. That’s the best!<br /><br />You also get a quick introduction to the hero of the next book, Valerius. I’m sure his will be a tortured and sad story — and I can’t wait to get to it. But alas, I will have to wait until the opportunity arises sometime next month. I know Valerius is another favorite. Really though, is there a man in this series who is not a favorite?!<br /><br />Seriously though, Vane deserves all of the *swoons* and daydreams he receives. “Night Play” is another well written and well paced installment in the Dark-Hunter series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2885091626076912075" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/160334544" />
    <a title="PepperP0t " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4859493-pepperp0t"><img alt="PepperP0t " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1566391632p2/4859493.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/160334544?book_show_action=true">Apr 11, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="PepperP0t " class="user" itemprop="url" name="PepperP0t " href="/user/show/4859493-pepperp0t">PepperP0t </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781429906142" href="/book/show/6981330-night-play">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4859493-pepperp0t?shelf=always-worth-re-reading">always-worth-re-reading</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4859493-pepperp0t?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4859493-pepperp0t?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4859493-pepperp0t?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4859493-pepperp0t?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4859493-pepperp0t?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4859493-pepperp0t?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4859493-pepperp0t?shelf=smexy-erotica">smexy-erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4859493-pepperp0t?shelf=snowed-in-with-only-this-book">snowed-in-with-only-this-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4859493-pepperp0t?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer160334544" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7819299721006206516">Arcadian were-hunter, Vane's is taken to task for his actions in Night Embrace. His brother Fang shares the cruel punishment doled out by the pack and they're left to fight for their lives or die. Unable to ever go home, Vane takes up residence in Sanctuary, run by the Peltier were-bear family with his comatose brother. <br/><br/>During his pity-party walk-about Vane, gets an up close and personal look at the delightful, quirky and image conscious Bride McTierney. For the second time, Vane wants nothing m</span>
  <span id="freeText7819299721006206516" style="display:none">Arcadian were-hunter, Vane's is taken to task for his actions in Night Embrace. His brother Fang shares the cruel punishment doled out by the pack and they're left to fight for their lives or die. Unable to ever go home, Vane takes up residence in Sanctuary, run by the Peltier were-bear family with his comatose brother. <br /><br />During his pity-party walk-about Vane, gets an up close and personal look at the delightful, quirky and image conscious Bride McTierney. For the second time, Vane wants nothing more than Bride but his insecurities over human fragility and inexperience with human females warn him keep his distance. Mmm...yummy. Vane's a sensitive hero that doesn't bother taking names when his protective, territorial alpha needs to clear a room.<br /><br />Bride has no memory of seeing Vane before but she's broken hearted since her live-in ex dumped her in a bizarrely humiliating way and no one has ever made her feel as beautiful and desirable as Vane does. Bride was a fun, funny kick a** heroine that just happens to have her own complementary hero cadre at her back. <br /><br />Bride's insecurities were a perfect foil for Vane's as they had different expectations of each other and see more positive qualities than negative. Vane's baggage includes danger as he reaches a sensitive crossroads with Bride and he has to figure out how to stay away and stay near at the same time. Entrusting those he has no reason to trust our intrepid hero has to make hard choices for both Bride and Fang<br /><br />Many new characters, including Fury, Otto, the Peltier family, Bride's Family and the characters in Sanctuary were added to the roster making the read feel overfull at times. Arcadian/Katagarian history slowed the pace in places. Humor &amp; wit were well used here and supplied some laugh out loud moments. The action was thrilling and did its bit to further the story. This fast paced read is fun times as some of the regulars also make appearances.<br /><br />Kenyon's storytelling skills kept Bride and Vane front and center for their HEA in this outing despite the amount of activity. For this reader's taste the story elements were firing on all cylinders, except the dryness of the Katagarians. Sanctuary will definitely be used in the future as a great place to settle warring faction issues in a small space and give the series a sense of cohesiveness. <br /><br />Originally date read/rated: 02/2012 - 4.75stars<br />This reading read/rating: 5stars</span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText7097389993525886095" style="display:none"><b>3,5/3<br>Seriye kurt-adam molasıııııı.</b><br><br>Yarı Katagaria yarı Arcadian olan Vane çiftleşmek için bir insan kadınıyla eşleşiyor bu kitapta.<br>Benim harika Julian’ım ve Karanlık Avcıları’mın hele hele Zarek'imin ardından beni yeterli oranda heyecanlandırmasa da güzel bir kitaptı.<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1493998118i/22674740.jpg" width="80" height="65" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <b>Wait!” she said as he touched the knob. “You left your necklace.”<br>Vane looked back at her one last time, knowing he would never see her again. She was so beautiful there with large, amber eyes set in the pale face of a goddess. There was something about her that reminded him of a Rubens angel. She was ethereal and lovely.<br>And far too fragile for an animal.<br>“No,” he said quietly. “I left it with the woman I wanted to have it.”</b>
</blockquote></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6QOZlEF6xX0A3TW7lUaEQ5k9gr/e0bFNBYESB7JsmHjTJfBG+iQMFaf2gdpis46cT2JldxBcPype/1S2fy9q4g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('j2BXILu9bxldowA7RCkcprsf96kv0Y9+FOqrKVoSZ+i1Rj7yAOOmcfqItFqz3BZ5bUAQYeFcARlPlO2Yl1GVcg==')})
  }
//]]>

Now both my mother and Morgen have decided that it\'s time I take my place on their side <\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText11957613435671290330\" style=\"display:none\">For countless centuries, I\'ve been the assassin for the infamous Merlin, even though the woman who birthed me sits at the right hand of our enemy, Morgen le Fey. Now both my mother and Morgen have decided that it\'s time I take my place on their side of this conflict.\n\nNormally, telling them no wouldn\'t be a problem, except for the fact that the good guys I protect think that I\'m an even worse demon than the ones we fight. Hmm, maybe they\'re right. I have to say that I do enjoy maiming anyone who gets in my way.\n\nAt least until my mother gives me a simple choice: join Morgen\'s Circle of the Damned or see an innocent woman die. I\'m all for saving the innocent, but Merewyn isn\'t as innocent as she seems. And she\'s none too fond of the fact that her fate is in my dubious hands. Personally I\'m all for taking the easy way out, but leaving her to Morgen is rough, even for me. Now the only way to save both our lives is to face the evilest forces ever known—my mother and Morgen. And two people who know nothing of trust must learn to rely on each other or die: provided we don\'t kill each other first.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"11957613435671290330\" href=\"#\"   <span id="freeText8280039863455748377" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.mysherrilyn.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Author site</a><br /><a href="http://crynevermore.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Nevermore site</a><br /><a href="http://www.deadmanscross.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Deadman's Cross site</a><br /><a href="http://www.sherrilynkenyon.com/book-series/chronicles-of-nick/" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Chronicles of Nick site</a><br /><a href="http://silentswans.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Silent Swans site</a><br /><a href="http://hunterlegends.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Hunter Legends site</a><br /><a href="http://witchofendor.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Witch of Endor site</a><br /><a href="http://Lordsofavalon.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Lords of Avalon site</a><br /><a href="http://www.facebook.com/AuthorSherrilynKenyon" rel="nofollow noopener">Official Facebook site</a><br /><br />New York Times and international bestselling author Sherrilyn Kenyon is a regular at the #1 spot. With legions of fans known as Paladins (thousands of whom proudly sport tattoos from her series and who travel from all over the world to attend her appearances), her books are always snatched up as soon as they appear on store shelves. Since 2004, she had placed more than 80 novels on the New York Times list in all formats including manga and graphic novels. Her current series are: Dark-Hunters, Chronicles of Nick and The League, and her books are available in over 100 countries where eager fans impatiently wait for the next release. Her Chronicles of Nick and Dark-Hunter series are soon to be major motion pictures while Dark-Hunter is also being developed as a television series.
